Giveaway ‚Äì $25 Walmart/Sam‚Äôs Club Gift Card!

   February 1, 2016 | [29]1,054 Comments

   [30]WalmartCard5 300

   The above is not what you will receive, your winning card will be from
   Sam‚Äôs Club. They are the same company and the gift cards are
   interchangeable between all their stores!

   GIVEAWAY:

   One lucky reader of the GayNYCDad award winning blog, will receive a
   $25 Sam‚Äôs Club Gift Card! This works at Walmart as well, they are owned
   by the same family!

   Mandatory Entries: Sign up for my blog via subscription and confirm
   your subscription! Leave a comment to tell that you have done so and
   the RSS feed does not count.

   Extra entries:
   1. Follow me on twitter [31]www.twitter.com/gaynycdad (click above
   right).
   2. Share this contest on your Facebook page using the button on the
   bottom of the post and share that link in your entry comment here.
   3. Retweet this info (you can use the tweet button at the bottom of the
   post) and leave me a comment with a link to your retweet.
   4. Retweet daily and leave a comment daily that you have done this.
   5. Extra entry for leaving a comment on a non-giveaway post ‚Äì you must
   leave a comment here as well to tell me that you have done so to get
   the entry.
   6. Visit[32] my Facebook page here, leave me a separate comment telling
   me you have done so.
   7. Follow me on [33]Instagram and leave a separate comment!
   8. Follow me on [34]Pinterest and leave a separate comment!
   9. Follow me on [35]Google Plus! And leave a separate comment!
   10. Subscribe to my [36]Youtube channel and leave me a comment here
   stating that you did!

   You must leave a separate comment in the comments field for each entry
   that you make to be entered! If you are already any of these things, to
   enter just leave a separate comment reminding me of that! Contest ends
   midnight, February 21, 2016. Prizes must be claimed within 48 hours.
   Maximum winnings of 2 giveaways per every 90 days. See [37]official
   rules for more information.

   Every entry requires a separate comment!

   Thanks and good-luck.
   Disclosure: I received no compensation for this post.
